# DOJ Epstein Files — Media Reference Index

> Source: https://www.justice.gov/epstein
> Total released: 3.5M pages, 180,000+ images, 2,000+ videos
> Release dates: Dec 19, 2025 (initial) → Jan 30, 2026 (major tranche)

---

## Access

| Resource | URL | Format |
|---------|-----|--------|
| DOJ Portal | https://www.justice.gov/epstein | HTML |
| Document search | https://www.justice.gov/epstein (search interface) | PDF, TIFF |
| EFTA documents | Searchable by EFTA reference number | PDF |

---

## Key EFTA References (Known)

| EFTA Code | Content | Format |
|-----------|---------|--------|
| EFTA00008744 | Scopolamine/devil's breath emails 2014–2015 | PDF/email |
| EFTA00666117 | Sultan bin Sulayem "torture video" email | PDF/email |

---

## Media File Types in DOJ Release

The DOJ release includes:
- `.pdf` — court documents, FBI reports, interview summaries
- `.jpg` / `.jpeg` — photographs (180,000+)
- `.tif` / `.tiff` — scanned documents
- `.mp4` / `.mov` / `.avi` — videos (2,000+)
- `.msg` / `.eml` — email files
- `.doc` / `.docx` — Word documents
- `.xls` / `.xlsx` — spreadsheets (financial records)

---

## Video Evidence Notes

- 2,000 videos released — nature/content not fully catalogued publicly
- FBI search warrant returns reference "video recordings" from properties
- Hidden camera footage — whether included in DOJ release is not confirmed
- Some videos appear to be surveillance or documentary; full index not public

---

## How to Reference DOJ Media in Vault

```markdown
![EFTA00008744 scopolamine email](https://www.justice.gov/epstein/...)
```

Or for local downloads:
```markdown
![[Media/EFTA00008744-scopolamine.pdf]]
```

- [ ] Download and locally cache key EFTA documents
- [ ] Index video files by subject/content as they are reviewed

- [ ] Track which documents are being redacted/withheld
